posted:Posted February 13, 2024
msg:I stayed at the Guangzhou Wanfu Hilton Hotel during the Chinese New Year. Overall, the hotel's services and facilities were very good, but there were some minor shortcomings.
First of all, the attitude of the hotel's service staff is very good. Especially Bettie. They were warm, friendly, attentive and thoughtful, which made me feel the high-quality service of Hilton brand. Whether it was the front desk, guest rooms or restaurants, the service staff were very professional and left a deep impression on me.
Secondly, the hotel room is very clean and tidy. The decoration and facilities in the room are very modern, and they are thoroughly cleaned every day, which made me feel very comfortable and at ease.
In addition, the hotel's breakfast is very rich and varied. The restaurant provides a variety of Chinese and Western breakfasts to meet the tastes of different guests.
However, there are some shortcomings. First of all, I felt uncomfortable with the square toilet in the hotel. I personally prefer a traditional round toilet, so this design is a bit unaccustomed to me.
Secondly, the hotel did not introduce me to the activities around the hotel during the Chinese New Year. As a visitor to Guangzhou for the New Year, I was very interested in Guangzhou's tourist attractions and surrounding activities, but the hotel did not provide information in this regard, which made me miss some wonderful experiences (the flower market next to the hotel was... They are demolishing).
In addition, I booked a hotel through Ctrip, but found that there were no Hilton points. As a frequent customer, I'm really looking forward to accumulating points and enjoying the corresponding benefits. It is hoped that the hotel can coordinate with Ctrip to ensure that the corresponding points can be obtained during the booking process.
Finally, the hotel is close to the airport, so the planes are noisy. Although the hotel has taken soundproofing measures, significant aircraft noise can still be heard at certain times, which affects rest.
Overall, the Guangzhou Wanfu Hilton Hotel is a hotel with very good services and facilities, but there are still some details that need to be improved. It is hoped that the hotel can continue to improve service quality and provide guests with a better stay experience.
